backend, and testing domains. At its foundation is the `.github/CODEOWNERS` file, which defines GitHub-level ownership rules mapping file patterns to individual owners or team references (e.g., @grafana/dataviz-squad). This file is validated by the CI workflow `.github/workflows/codeowners-validator.yml`, which runs the mszostok/codeowners-validator action to check for syntax errors, invalid owners, and duplicate patterns on every pull request.\\n\\nThe codeowners-manifest infrastructure bridges the gap between the CODEOWNERS file and internal tooling. The `toggles_gen_test.go` test suite validates feature flag configurations and generates three machine-readable outputs: (1) `toggles_gen.go` - exported Go constants and functions; (2) `toggles_gen.json` - Kubernetes-style FeatureList resource with metadata and codeowner in the spec; and (3) `toggles_gen.csv` - CSV export for documentation.
